3. The daily_proactive_limit is per-agent-config and is stored in agent_configs table with FK to agents (1:1 relationship). Each agent has its own limit setting:
   - dispatcher.ts:320-323: `const dailyLimit = typeof agentConfig?.daily_proactive_limit === "number" && agentConfig.daily_proactive_limit > 0 ? agentConfig.daily_proactive_limit : 0;`
   - The agentConfig is fetched by rule.agent_id (line 247-251)

4. While the query on line 326-331 does count ALL proactives to a rep without filtering by agent_id, this is architecturally immaterial because:
   - In V2 (production now), there is 1 Sparkbot global (cron comment line 71-72)
   - Only that one agent generates rules
   - There is no scenario where multiple account_assistants simultaneously fire to same rep in current architecture
   - The comment explicitly states expectation of single Sparkbot: "V2: 1 Sparkbot global" (line 360)

The described scenario (Sales Agent A exhausting limit) is impossible because Sales Agent is not involved in proactive rules at all. References: src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/dispatcher.ts:314-341, src/app/api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:71-76, supabase/migrations/00082_agents_allow_multi_custom.sql:19-21
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] outbound_to_contact silently falls back from WhatsApp to SMS** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: If WhatsApp subscription inactive, send_message_to_contact silently retries SMS without user awareness. Recipient sees SMS instead of WhatsApp (different UX, user confusion, potential deliverability issues on SMS side). Rep doesn't know delivery channel changed.
  - Fix: Add channel confirmation note in sparkbot_messages audit trail: 'Msg scheduled for WhatsApp, sent via SMS (API unavailable)'. Surface to rep in web UI if they check delivery status. Emit signal if fallback happens for 'mission-critical' outbound (contact_id in blacklist/VIP list).
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] No graceful degradation if pg_cron lock acquisition fails** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: pg_try_advisory_xact_lock(8675309) is assumed to always succeed. If lock contention is extreme (multiple cron workers competing) or if pg_cron backend is overloaded, lock could timeout or be unavailable. Code has no retry logic or circuit breaker — would fail the entire cron tick.
  - Fix: Wrap lock acquisition in retry loop (3 attempts, 100ms exponential backoff). If lock fails all retries, emit signal and skip tick (preferential to crashing). Add histogram metric 'lock_acquisition_latency_ms' for observability. Test under simulated contention.


---

## SparkBot — billing, onboarding & termos

SparkBot's billing system tracks usage via `usage_records` table with support for multi-modal costs (LLM tokens, audio, cache, images). It enforces a monthly spend cap (default $100/location, NULL=unlimited) and skips charges when cap is reached while keeping the bot responsive. Terms flow uses `parseTermsResponse` with LGPD-compliant negation detection, persisting acceptance/rejection in `rep_identities`. Onboarding auto-confirms timezone from GHL location data. Internal team detection (env phones, GHL role, 5+ locations heuristic) exempts from charges via `usesCustomKey` semantics. Billing relies on atomic claim-based retry with 15min reaper for stale claims.

### Funcionalidades

**Pricing & Cost Calculation — 9/10**
- ✅ Comprehensive pricing.ts covers Claude/OpenAI models with accurate cache pricing (10% read, 125% write for Anthropic). SafeToken calculations prevent double-counting cached vs fresh input. Markup 10% applied correctly. Format helpers for readable USD display.
- ⚠️ GPT-5.4 pricing is placeholder (models not officially released). DEFAULT_PRICING fallback to gpt-4.1-mini may mask unknown model changes in production. No dynamic pricing update mechanism if GHL API pricing changes.
- 🔧 Add model version tracking and pricing version in usage_records. Implement alerts if unknown model is encountered >N times/day. Document fallback strategy for new OpenAI model releases.

**Usage Tracking & Recording — 8/10**
- ✅ Migration 00056 fixed critical schema drift (cached_tokens, cache_creation_tokens, audio_seconds, image_count, claim_token columns now exist). insertUsageRecord handles all multi-modal dimensions. Idempotency via usage_record.id for GHL wallet calls. Error handling via console.error; doesn't block processing.
- ⚠️ insertUsageRecord silently returns null on error instead of throwing—callers must check. No validation that usage_record.id was returned before proceeding to markWalletCharged. Potential race: if INSERT partially fails but charging proceeds anyway.
- 🔧 Add explicit error logging with record details (model, tokens, cost) to Sentry/admin_signals. Validate record.id !== null before charge attempt. Add instrumentation counter for failed inserts vs successful charges.

**Monthly Spend Cap Enforcement — 7/10**
- ✅ Cap logic is sound: looks up MIN of all agent_configs.monthly_spend_cap_usd per location (no agent escapes by configuring its own), sums monthly spend correctly (EXCLUDING cap_blocked), skips charge when exceeded but bot continues (UX preserved). Marked cap_blocked=true for audit. Index idx_usage_records_unbilled_capready avoids retry of capped records.
- ⚠️ isMonthlyCapReached uses `startOfMonth` set to UTC 00:00:00—does not account for location timezone. Location in Hawaii sees cap reset 10 hours before rep in Florida. Monthly cycle is calendar-driven not rolling. Cap is location-level, not per-agent or per-rep (one spender hitting cap silences everyone).
- 🔧 Use location.timezone to compute startOfMonth in rep's local time. Consider rolling 30-day window option. Add per-rep spending dashboard visibility before cap is hit so rep can self-limit. Alert admin at 80% cap threshold.

**Billing Retry & Atomic Claim — 8/10**
- ✅ Two-step atomic claim (SELECT ids→UPDATE by ids) is correct pattern to bound batch size and prevent unbounded lambda timeouts. Reaper for stale claims (>15min unclaimed or claimed but uncharged) prevents deadlock. Bounded batch size 40 fits in 60s lambda. Concurrency-safe via claim_token UUID per execution.
- ⚠️ Reaper runs EVERY chargeUnbilledRecords call but 15min cutoff is hard-coded (not configurable). If a single charge takes >15min, the reaper incorrectly releases it before processing completes. No backoff strategy—failed record retried on NEXT cron (5min interval) immediately, may hammer same GHL 400 error again.
- 🔧 Make reaper cutoff configurable in cron_config table. Add exponential backoff: 1st fail=5min, 2nd=15min, 3rd+=60min via claimed_at+retry_count columns. Log failed chargeId so admin can correlate GHL-side issues.

**Internal Team Detection — 7/10**
- ✅ Three-layer detection (env INTERNAL_TEAM_PHONES, GHL role='agency', heuristic 5+ locations) is robust. Async syncRepInternalFlag is idempotent (updates only on change). Billing treats internal as usesCustomKey (tracked but not charged). Audit trail preserved in usage_records.
- ⚠️ Detection happens AFTER trackAndCharge called in processor.ts:688—if syncRepInternalFlag fails, `isInternal` defaults to true (fails safe), but default should be documented. Env list parsing does not validate E.164 format (malformed phones silently ignored). Heuristic '5+ locations' may incorrectly flag power users in small agencies.
- 🔧 Move internal detection BEFORE trackAndCharge, cache result in rep object to avoid re-detection per turn. Validate E.164 format in env parsing. Make 5+ threshold configurable per location. Log internal status change in execution_log for audit.

**Terms Acceptance & Rejection — 9/10**
- ✅ parseTermsResponse has excellent LGPD logic: NEGATION_PATTERN checked BEFORE ACCEPT (fails safe). 'Não tá ok pra mim' correctly maps to REJECT. STRONG_REFUSAL patterns catch explicit refusals anywhere in text. Suffix strip handles interactive button metadata. Yes-but-no ('aceito que errei mas não concordo') → unclear, re-asks. Migration 00052 persists terms_rejected_at to silence bot.
- ⚠️ normalizeForParse strips diacritics globally—'não' becomes 'nao'—works but is lossy. NEGATION_PATTERN is loose regex (/\b(nao|...)/); false positive risk if rep says 'eu nao tenho nada pra dizer' (should be accept-adjacent context, not rejection). ACCEPT_KEYWORDS match is strict (only start or whole-word), rejecting 'ok vou aceitar' → unclear.
- 🔧 Add context window check for NEGATION_PATTERN (negation valid only if near start or after punctuation). Expand ACCEPT_KEYWORDS to include 'vou aceitar', 'pode contar comigo'. Add telemetry counter for parseTermsResponse outcomes (accept/reject/unclear ratios) to detect LGPD logic drift.

**Onboarding & Timezone Confirmation — 9/10**
- ✅ buildOnboardingForWhatsApp auto-reads location.timezone from GHL (no rep friction). formatTimezoneHumanFriendly maps IANA→city + DST abbrev. confirmTimezoneFromLocation idempotent (only updates if timezone_confirmed_at is null, respects manual override). Onboarding message has rich examples + interactive buttons. Schema migration 00046 creates timezone columns.
- ⚠️ formatTimezoneHumanFriendly uses Intl.DateTimeFormat for abbrev which reflects NOW; if location is set EDT but rep in EST (off-season), abbrev is wrong until next DST boundary. Fallback city name parsing (last part of IANA) is dumb—'America/Argentina/Sao_Paulo' becomes 'Sao Paulo' not 'Buenos Aires'.
- 🔧 Use date-fns getTimezoneOffset or ICU DateTimeFormat with specific date to reflect actual offset. Expand TZ_CITY_MAP to include Argentina zones. Add button to re-confirm timezone if rep says 'mudei pra ...' (tool confirm_rep_timezone exists but onboarding doesn't prompt).

**Multi-modal Cost Components (Audio, Images, Cache) — 8/10**
- ✅ Audio tracking: audioSeconds + audioModel persisted in usage_records migration 00056. Whisper billing called in webhook-handler.ts when audioSink.current is populated. Cache tracking: cachedTokens + cacheCreationTokens with correct Anthropic 125% premium. Image telemetry: image_count column tracks vision calls.
- ⚠️ Audio tracking only happens for Whisper transcription in webhook-handler (line 659–686); if another LLM call uses audio downstream (e.g., Sonnet vision), THOSE tokens are NOT tagged as audio_seconds (double-count risk or under-billing). Image count is logged in metadata but NOT passed to trackAndCharge—Vision billing completely missing in LLM calls.
- 🔧 Pass image_count, audioSeconds from result.metadata into trackAndCharge for ALL LLM calls. Separate audio_model from vision_model in usage_records. Add test: call Sonnet with image→verify image_count and cost reflect Vision pricing.

**BYO API Key / Custom Key Flow — 7/10**
- ✅ location_settings.openai_api_key is checked before transcribe (webhook-handler:424–429) and Whisper uses it if present. markCustomKeyCharged marks usage as tracked but not charged. processor.ts correctly passes usesCustomKey=isInternal to billing.
- ⚠️ BYO key for LLM inference is NOT implemented—processor.ts ignores location_settings for Anthropic/OpenAI token billing. Only Whisper respects BYO key. Rep with custom OpenAI key will have BOTH Whisper and LLM calls charged to Pedro's wallet (partial workaround doesn't work).
- 🔧 Add location_settings.anthropic_api_key column (migration). Pass into processIncoming so LLM calls use customer key if set. Mark usage_records with uses_custom_key=true. Document BYO key setup in onboarding.

**Billing Observability & Alerts — 6/10**
- ✅ chargeUnbilledRecords returns {charged, failed, reaped, errors[]} with sample errors logged. Console.warn for stale unbilled alerts (>1h old). Cap check logs spend/cap/newCharge on block. execution_log records action_type='account_assistant_turn' with token breakdown.
- ⚠️ Errors array is capped at 5 samples (line 296–298)—on mass failure, only 5 record IDs surfaced. No structured logging to Sentry; relying on Vercel logs. Failed charges (400 GHL errors) are silently retried without circuit-breaker. No dashboard showing cap utilization per location. Monthly billing report endpoint (/api/billing) is not audited for data freshness.
- 🔧 Send billing errors to admin_signals table + Sentry with location_id+model breakdown. Add circuit-breaker: disable billing cron if >50% of chargeWallet calls fail in last hour. Build cap utilization widget in /hub/billing. Implement billing reconciliation job comparing usage_records vs GHL Marketplace charges.

**Terms Persistence & Reset — 8/10**
- ✅ terms_accepted_at and terms_rejected_at are discrete columns in rep_identities. processor.ts checks !rep.terms_accepted_at && rep.terms_rejected_at → silence (fails safe). Comment in 00052 documents admin reset: UPDATE rep_identities SET terms_rejected_at = NULL. acceptTerms/rejectTerms in identity.ts call setTermsAccepted/setTermsRejected (repos).
- ⚠️ No expiration logic—once terms_accepted_at is set, rep NEVER re-accepts (could be outdated TOS). terms_rejected_at silences forever with no built-in unlock (admin must know to run raw SQL). No audit log of who reset terms or when. No webhook/notification if many reps reject.
- 🔧 Add terms_version to terms_accepted_at logic; if terms change, auto-re-prompt reps who accepted old version. Allow reps to self-reset rejection after N days. Log admin resets in execution_log. Track rejection reasons (optional form after 'no') to improve TOS.

### Structural issues
- **[MEDIUM] Dead/Incomplete Code: checkWalletBalance is Stubbed and Never Called** — charge.ts lines 213–221 define checkWalletBalance that always returns true with a TODO comment. Function is imported nowhere and never called. Suggests abandoned wallet balance pre-check feature. If intended, creates false impression that wallet solvency is verified. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/billing/charge.ts)
- **[HIGH] Usage Reporting Endpoints Missing or Undocumented** — usage-records.repo.ts exports sumUsageCosts, getUsageBreakdown, getLocationBillingRecords but no API routes are visible in codebase. Assumed endpoint /api/billing exists (line 125 comment) but no route file found. Dashboard may not be showing real billing data to admin. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/repositories/usage-records.repo.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] Whisper Billing Only in Webhook, Not in Test Routes or Proactive Dispatcher** — webhook-handler.ts lines 659–686 charge Whisper. But /api/agents/account-assistant/test/route.ts may call transcriber without charging (testSessionId check happens AFTER transcribe). Proactive dispatcher calls LLM but may not track all audio if re-transcribed. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/account-assistant/webhook-handler.ts)
- **[HIGH] Image Count Telemetry Not Wired to Billing** — webhook-handler.ts:862 stores image_count in metadata but never extracts it for trackAndCharge. Vision API is called in processIncoming but result doesn't include image_count in the return type. Metadata is JSON—extracting image_count requires parsing, which isn't done. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/account-assistant/webhook-handler.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] Migration 00056 May Silently Fail on Old DB — Missing error signal** — 00056 uses IF NOT EXISTS on column ALTERs. If Supabase auto-created usage_records from SETUP.sql with wrong schema, the migration succeeds but columns remain uninitialized (defaulted to 0 or null). No signal to admin that billing is now broken. chargeUnbilledRecords will use defaults (cached_tokens=0, image_count=0) leading to under-billing. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/supabase/migrations/00056_usage_records_schema_drift_recovery.sql)
- **[LOW] Circular Dependency Risk: processor.ts imports billing, billing queries agents repo** — processor.ts → charge.ts → agents.repo.ts → agents table. No cycle, but dependency chain is long. If agents.repo.getLocationSpendCap fails, the catch in processor.ts (line 688) silently defaults to internal (blocks charge instead of propagating error). (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] No Validation of Cap Values—Zero or Negative Caps Possible** — agent_configs.monthly_spend_cap_usd is numeric(10, 2) with no CHECK constraint. Admin could set cap to -100 or 0. isMonthlyCapReached checks `!Number.isFinite(capUsd) || capUsd <= 0` but gracefully ignores (treats as no cap). Should reject or log warning. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/supabase/migrations/00049_monthly_spend_cap.sql)
- **[LOW] Stale Records Index Performance Not Optimized** — idx_usage_records_unbilled_capready (migration 00056) is excellent but findStaleUnbilledRecords uses no index. Query filters on charged_to_wallet=false + uses_custom_key=false + total_charge_usd>0 + created_at<cutoff. Missing composite index (charged_to_wallet, uses_custom_key, created_at DESC) would speed alert scanning on large tables. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/repositories/usage-records.repo.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] No Soft Delete or TTL for Usage Records—Unbounded Table Growth** — usage_records has no TTL, archive strategy, or soft-delete. After 1 year of 100k turns/day = 36M rows. getMonthlySpend query will scan full table with index. No retention policy documented. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/supabase/migrations/00040_usage_records_and_drift_recovery.sql)
- **[LOW] Terms Interactive Payload Text Not Localized** — buildTermsInteractive/TERMS_OF_USE_TEXT are hard-coded in PT-BR with no i18n. If Brazillionaires expands to EN market, terms will be in Portuguese only. Button labels 'Aceito ✅' / 'Não aceito ❌' are not configurable. (/Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/account-assistant/terms.ts)

### Production blockers
- **[CONFIRMED/HIGH] Image & Vision Billing Completely Missing from LLM Tracking** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: processor.ts calls trackAndCharge with promptTokens/completionTokens/cachedTokens but NEVER passes imageCount or vision_model. If a turn uses Claude Sonnet vision (analyze image, transcribe form, etc.), the image_count is logged in metadata but not billed. Result: Pedro gives away Vision inference ($0.001-0.003/image) for free while thinking it's being charged.
  - Fix: Add image_count, vision_model fields to result object from processIncoming/LLM calls. Pass to trackAndCharge in processor.ts line 690+. Update usage-records.repo.ts insertUsageRecord to store these. Add test call with vision to verify billing reflects image cost.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts:690-705 — trackAndCharge call is missing imageCount parameter. The call passes only: locationId, companyId, agentId, contactId, actionType, model, promptTokens, completionTokens, cachedTokens, cacheCreationTokens, usesCustomKey. imageCount is NOT included.

src/lib/billing/charge.ts:17-32 — TrackUsageParams interface defines imageCount?: number at line 30 with comment "// telemetria de vision", and line 72 shows it's inserted into usage_records as image_count: params.imageCount ?? 0. This field is OPTIONAL and defaults to 0 when not provided.

src/lib/billing/pricing.ts:119-174 — calculateCost function has NO vision/image pricing logic. Lines 156-159 show ONLY audio pricing is calculated. There is NO VISION_PRICING table or imageCount parameter in the cost calculation. The comment at line 111 says "- audio: audioSeconds × AUDIO_PRICING[model]" with no mention of images.

src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts:854-938 (buildUserMessage) — When input.kind === "image", the function builds an LLMMessage with image content (lines 928-937), but this image data is NEVER counted or tracked after the LLM processes it.

src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts:125-127 — The processIncoming function receives the input parameter with input.input accessible, which contains kind field that identifies image inputs. This data is available at line 690 where trackAndCharge is called but is never used.
- **[REFUTED/LOW] Cached Tokens & Cache Creation Tokens May Be Miscalculated in Safe Dedup Logic** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: pricing.ts calculateCost has safeCached/safeCacheCreation logic to prevent double-counting. But the logic assumes cachedT + cacheCreationT ≤ promptT. If a call reports cachedTokens=5000 + cacheCreationTokens=3000 + promptTokens=6000, the safe logic forces cacheCreationT = Math.min(3000, 6000-5000) = 1000, losing 2000 tokens. Per Anthropic docs, cached + fresh should sum to total prompt.
  - Fix: Review lines 147–149 in pricing.ts. Add assertion/log if safeCached+safeCacheCreation > promptTokens. Check llm-client.ts to understand how Anthropic SDK returns cache_read vs cache_creation vs input_tokens and ensure they are summed correctly before passing to calculateCost.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/billing/pricing.ts:113-117 documents the API contract: "Anthropic SDK retorna cache_creation_input_tokens e cache_read_input_tokens SEPARADOS de input_tokens. llm-client.ts soma todos em prompt_tokens pra normalizar com OpenAI; então aqui descontamos ambos do fresh pra evitar double count." The Anthropic SDK types (@anthropic-ai/sdk/resources/beta/messages/messages.d.ts) explicitly state: "Total input tokens in a request is the summation of input_tokens, cache_creation_input_tokens, and cache_read_input_tokens." This means the scenario (cachedT=5000, cacheCreationT=3000, promptT=6000) is impossible per API contract—promptT must equal freshInput+5000+3000=8000. With valid inputs (promptT=8000, cachedT=5000, cacheCreationT=3000), lines 147-149 correctly compute: safeCached=5000, safeCacheCreation=3000, freshInputTokens=0, total=8000. The 2026-05-26 ultra-review (C3-SINTESE.md:61) explicitly evaluated this and marked it as false-positive ("Double-count de cached...Correto"). However, a DIFFERENT bug (C3-3, C3-SINTESE.md:47-52) exists: cache_creation_tokens are never actually populated/persisted in practice (always 0), so when eventually exposed they would be billed correctly at 125% per the logic, but currently they never flow through the system.
- **[CONFIRMED/HIGH] Monthly Spend Cap Ignores Location Timezone—Uses UTC** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: isMonthlyCapReached line 251–253 computes startOfMonth as UTC 00:00. Location in Hawaii resets cap 10 hours before location in Florida. If Pedro set $100 cap for all Brazillionaires locations, a Hawaii-based agent burns $100, gets capped, then 10 hours later Florida agent starts fresh day with cap reset. Confusing for reps.
  - Fix: Fetch location.timezone in isMonthlyCapReached. Adjust startOfMonth to local midnight: `new Date(new Date().toLocaleString('en-US', { timeZone: location.timezone })).setHours(0,0,0,0)`. Or use date-fns startOfDay with timezone parameter.
  - Veredicto: /src/lib/billing/charge.ts:250-257 — `isMonthlyCapReached` calculates `startOfMonth` via `new Date(); .setDate(1); .setHours(0,0,0,0)` then `.toISOString()`. This approach ALWAYS produces a fixed UTC boundary regardless of location timezone. JavaScript `.setHours()` operates in the SERVER'S local timezone, then `.toISOString()` converts to UTC. On the actual server (confirmed via node execution), this produces "2026-06-01T04:00:00.000Z" (0 hours EDT = 4 hours UTC). The function queries `getMonthlySpend(locationId, startOfMonth.toISOString())` which filters `created_at >= 2026-06-01T04:00:00Z` for ALL locations. However, `/supabase/migrations/00001_create_locations.sql:7` defines `timezone TEXT DEFAULT 'America/New_York'` but this column is NEVER consulted by `isMonthlyCapReached`. Different locations (Hawaii UTC-10, Florida UTC-4, Brazil UTC-3) will have "month start" at different actual local times, causing cap reset anomalies. Example: Hawaii 2026-05-31 18:00 HST = 2026-06-01 04:00 UTC (counts toward June cap), but locally it's still May 31. No timezone handling in the entire `charge.ts` or `usage-records.repo.ts` billing stack.
- **[PARTIAL/HIGH] Internal Team Detection Defaults to True on syncRepInternalFlag Failure** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: processor.ts line 688: `const isInternal = await syncRepInternalFlag(rep).catch(() => rep.is_internal === true);` — if syncRepInternalFlag throws (DB error, etc.), it defaults to treating the rep as internal, SKIPPING the charge. In production DB outages, all turns become free. Should fail open to charging, not closed.
  - Fix: Change catch to `return rep.is_internal ?? false;` (use cached value if error, default to false). Add console.error logging for the exception. Consider 3-tier fallback: cached → env list → charge it.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts:688 — `const isInternal = await syncRepInternalFlag(rep).catch(() => rep.is_internal === true);`

The fallback does NOT default to true universally. It returns `rep.is_internal === true` (a boolean comparison), which means:
- If rep.is_internal is already true in DB: returns true ✓ (safe fallback)
- If rep.is_internal is false in DB: returns false ✗ (CHARGES when should skip)

For new reps, rep.is_internal defaults to false (supabase/migrations/00048_rep_internal_flag.sql line 20). If syncRepInternalFlag fails on first sync (DB outage), the rep is marked as external and charged, opposite to the claim.

Example: Pedro (internal) makes first turn → identifyRep() creates rep with is_internal=false → syncRepInternalFlag() UPDATE fails → fallback evaluates `false === true` = false → usesCustomKey=false → trackAndCharge() calls chargeWallet() (line 704-705, charge.ts:88-90).

Real issue: fails OPEN to charging for internal team when DB is unhealthy, not closed. Claim inverts the actual behavior.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] chargeUnbilledRecords Reaper Has Hard-Coded 15min Cutoff Without Bounds** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: If a single chargeWallet call takes >15min (network hung, GHL slow), the reaper will release the claim_token before processing finishes. On next cron, claimUnbilledBatch re-claims the same record and duplicate-charges it (eventId idempotency in GHL should catch this, but no guarantee). No backoff or exponential retry; failed record retried immediately on next cron.
  - Fix: Add retry_count column to usage_records. In reapStaleClaims, only release if claimed_at + 15min < now() AND retry_count < 5. In chargeUnbilledRecords catch block, increment retry_count and increase claimed_at by exponential backoff (2^retry_count * 5min). Log to admin_signals if retry_count > 3.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Billing for LLM Turns May Not Respect BYO API Key—Only Whisper Does** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: location_settings.openai_api_key is passed to Whisper transcriber (webhook-handler:429) but NOT to the LLM inference in processor.ts. Rep with custom OpenAI key gets charged for both their Whisper usage AND their LLM tokens (should be free if they provided key). Feature incomplete.
  - Fix: Add location_settings.anthropic_api_key migration column. Load location_settings at start of processIncoming. If anthropic_api_key is set, use it in llm-client.ts instead of env key. Mark usage_records uses_custom_key=true if either key is set. Document setup in web UI.


---

## Ferramentas — registry, confirmation gate & test mode

95 tools organized across 18 categories (contacts, messages, calendar, notes, tasks, opportunities, reminders, etc.), with 3-level risk classification (safe=47, medium=29, high=19). Critical H8 confirmation gate enforced at runtime in executeTool(): tools marked medium/high risk require confirmed_by_rep:true flag after verbal rep confirmation. Test mode gate (testSessionId check) mocks non-safe tools to prevent production CRM modifications during testing. withConfirmationParam() injects the flag dynamically into schemas based on confirmation_mode (always/medium_and_high/high_only), ensuring LLM has proper parameter binding.

### Funcionalidades

**Tool Registry & Definition Management — 9/10**
- ✅ All 95 tools consolidated in index.ts with single source of truth. Tool entries standardized (def + handler). Risk levels consistently defined. Helper functions for validation (validateGhlId, validateIso8601, ghlErrorToResult) prevent common input/output errors.
- ⚠️ No explicit registry validation on startup (e.g., checking for duplicate tool names, undefined handlers). Tools added to REGISTRY via simple map — no integrity check.
- 🔧 Add startup validation: ensure every tool in ALL_ENTRIES has unique name + valid handler + defined risk level. Optionally generate tool inventory docs from registry.

**H8 Confirmation Gate — Schema Injection — 9/10**
- ✅ withConfirmationParam() correctly clones tool definitions and injects confirmed_by_rep field based on confirmation_mode. Field marked REQUIRED in schema (fixes GPT-4.1 fallback issue where LLM omitted the field). Description clearly explains first call (false) → rep verbal confirm → second call (true) flow. getAllToolDefinitions/getToolDefinitions properly gate tool set before passing to LLM.
- ⚠️ No validation that injected confirmed_by_rep doesn't conflict with existing tool params. If a tool accidentally already defines confirmed_by_rep, injection silently skips (line 102 check), potentially hiding a bug.
- 🔧 Warn if a tool defines confirmed_by_rep manually. Add test ensuring injected param is present in schema before LLM sees it.

**H8 Confirmation Gate — Runtime Enforcement — 10/10**
- ✅ executeTool() checks requiresConfirm before handler execution (line 218). Matches risk + confirmation_mode correctly. Returns retryable:true error directing LLM to ask 'Confirma?' then re-call with flag. Flag removed before handler (line 233) so handlers don't see it. Flow gates test mode BEFORE confirmation, preventing test-mode bypass of confirmation check.
- ⚠️ None identified. Gate is solid.
- 🔧 Optional: log/metric on how often confirmation gate blocks, to measure rep friction vs. safety tradeoff.

**Test Mode Gate — 9/10**
- ✅ Test mode gate (line 197) executes FIRST, before confirmation. Checks testSessionId && testSessionId.length > 0 && risk !== 'safe' (not just truthy testSessionId). Returns {simulated:true, ...} with args_preview for debugging. Preserves read-only tools (risk='safe') to allow analysis chains in test.
- ⚠️ testSessionId field in ToolContext is optional but not strongly typed (string | null vs explicit discriminator). Empty string check length > 0 is correct but could be clearer (e.g., constants.MIN_SESSIONID_LENGTH).
- 🔧 Consider TypeScript discriminated union for test vs. prod mode. Add integration test: schedule_reminder in test mode should return {simulated:true}, not actually insert into DB.

**Risk Classification Accuracy — 8/10**
- ✅ High-risk tools (19) correctly include destructive ops (delete_*, cancel_*) and outbound communication (send_message_to_contact, schedule_message_to_contact, schedule_bulk_message_v2). Medium-risk (29) correctly includes creation/modification (create_*, update_*, add_tag, create_note, etc.). Safe read-only tools (47) cover searches, listings, previews. Logic in toolRequiresConfirmation() matches risk levels.
- ⚠️ Few edge cases: cancel_reminder is safe (correct—it's rep's own reminder), but inconsistent naming might confuse auditors. remove_tag is medium (correct), but users might expect it medium like add_tag is. No single source of truth document explaining risk rationale for each tool.
- 🔧 Add comments in tool defs explaining WHY a tool is marked as its risk level, esp. for non-obvious ones. Consider doc: `_planning/tool-risk-classification.md` with audit trail.

**GHL Error Handling & Sanitization — 9/10**
- ✅ ghlErrorToResult() extracts status codes + messages, sanitizes URLs/IDs/traceIds (lines 184-193), exposes meaningful messages to LLM without leaking inter-tenant info. Special case: duplicate contact errors extract contactId + name, guiding LLM to update_contact. Code/5xx errors marked retryable:true. 403 errors correctly classified as scope_or_location code for governance.
- ⚠️ Sanitization regex might miss some URL patterns (e.g., data: URIs, gopher://, etc.), though unrealistic for GHL responses. Error extraction from JSON assumes valid JSON after 'GHL API {code}:' prefix — malformed responses might not extract cleanly.
- 🔧 Add fallback: if JSON extraction fails, try structured error object from GHL SDK (if available). Log redacted full error for debug without exposing to rep.

**Input Validation (GHL IDs, ISO8601, etc.) — 8/10**
- ✅ validateGhlId() rejects short IDs, all-numeric (phone), all-same-char patterns (aaaaaa), enforces 18+ chars + alphanumeric only. validateIso8601() checks Date constructor + timezone format. resolveAssignedUserId() handles 'self'/'me'/'eu' keywords + validates UUID-like user IDs. Helpers consistently used across tools.
- ⚠️ validateGhlId regex !/^[A-Za-z0-9]+$/ excludes hyphens, but some GHL IDs might use them (though real GHL IDs are uppercase-mixed alphanumeric). No explicit rejection of obviously fake IDs like '12345678901234567' (18 chars but suspiciously regular pattern).
- 🔧 Add fuzz test: attempt to pass known-fake IDs + confirm rejection. Document GHL ID format spec referenced by validateGhlId().

**Tool Executor Integration (buildToolCtx, runSparkbotTurn) — 9/10**
- ✅ buildToolCtx() helper centralizes ToolContext assembly. runSparkbotTurn() in core/run-sparkbot-turn.ts selects tools (all vs subset), passes confirmationMode correctly, includes F58 dedup of identical CREATE tools in same turn (preventing duplicate task/reminder creation). Executor patterns match processor.ts + dispatcher.ts.
- ⚠️ F58 dedup only covers IDEMPOTENT_CREATE_TOOLS set — if a new destructive CREATE is added and forgotten in set, no dedup coverage. No warning/error if set is stale vs actual tools.
- 🔧 Generate IDEMPOTENT_CREATE_TOOLS from tool registry annotations (add flag idempotent:true to ToolDefinition) instead of hardcoding. Add test: verify dedup works for all marked-idempotent tools.

**Disabled Tools Configuration — 8/10**
- ✅ getAllToolDefinitions() + getToolDefinitions() both accept disabledNames parameter, filtering out admin-disabled tools before passing to LLM. processor.ts uses this to hide present_options when STEVO_INTERACTIVE_ENABLED=false. integrates with agent_configs.disabled_tools from DB.
- ⚠️ No validation that disabledNames contains actual tool names — passing ['nonexistent_tool'] silently succeeds. No audit log of which tools were disabled for which rep/location/turn.
- 🔧 Validate disabledNames against TOOL_REGISTRY.keys(). Log when tools are disabled via admin config.

**Schema Parameter Binding (confirmed_by_rep Field) — 9/10**
- ✅ confirmed_by_rep injected into parameters.properties + marked required (line 119-121). Description explicitly guides LLM (pass false 1st, ask 'Confirma?', pass true 2nd). Prevents LLM from forgetting the field (seen in prod with GPT-4.1 fallback before fix).
- ⚠️ No check that required field is actually enforced client-side by LLM SDK (Anthropic/OpenAI might not validate). If SDK allows omitting required fields, gate becomes suggestion not enforcement.
- 🔧 Add unit test: mock LLM omitting confirmed_by_rep on high-risk tool → confirm executeTool() returns error + LLM retries. Verify both Anthropic + OpenAI SDKs enforce required params.

**Multi-Tenancy & Security Isolation — 8/10**
- ✅ validateGhlId() checks contact belongs to location (cross-tenant filter in search_conversations lines 40-42). ghlErrorToResult() sanitizes locationId/companyId from errors. ToolContext binds rep + locationId + companyId. Tools use these to enforce rep.id != other_rep_id (e.g., cancel_reminder line 288).
- ⚠️ No explicit audit of every tool to ensure contact_id/opportunity_id/etc filters respect location_id. Some tools might fetch data cross-location if GHL API has gaps. createAppointment (line 1016) validates IDs but doesn't check if contact belongs to active location.
- 🔧 Scan all tools for location-binding: ensure GHL API call includes locationId. Add integration test: rep from location A tries to modify contact from location B → must fail.

**Error Handling & Retry Logic — 7/10**
- ✅ ghlErrorToResult() marks 429 + 5xx retryable:true. handlers wrap GHL calls in try/catch. Most tools return consistent {status, message, retryable} shape. Signal auto-recording on non-retryable errors (lines 271-285).
- ⚠️ Some error messages generic ('Spark Leads rejeitou X') when GHL message is unavailable. No exponential backoff retry in executeTool — caller (processor) must handle. No circuit breaker if GHL is down (tool keeps failing).
- 🔧 Add context.retryCount + backoff in executeTool for retryable errors. Monitor: track 5xx error rates per tool/location.

### Structural issues
- **[HIGH] send_message_to_contact Risk Level Inconsistency** — send_message_to_contact is marked risk:high (correct), but the description (line 111) says 'SEMPRE peça confirmação ANTES' while schedule_message_to_contact (which is also high) has identical language. However, looking at the messages.ts file, send_message_to_contact is high but schedule_message_to_contact is also high (line 244). This is CORRECT, but the tool names could be clearer: sending NOW vs scheduling is clear semantically but in Portuguqese the wording is nearly identical, risk of rep misunderstanding which tool was called. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/messages.ts:107-112, 239-244)
- **[HIGH] delete_appointment Risk Level — Should Be High, Currently Safe** — delete_appointment (calendar.ts line ~1463) is marked risk:safe, but deletion of a scheduled appointment is destructive and could break customer communication (e.g., meeting was supposed to happen but bot deletes the calendar slot). This should be risk:high to require confirmation. Current: safe. Expected: high. Impact: rep or bot could accidentally delete customer appointments without confirmation. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/calendar.ts (line where delete_appointment is defined))
- **[HIGH] Missing Delete Confirmation Gates for Destructive Read-Only-Appearing Tools** — Several tools are marked safe but perform deletions or modifications: delete_note (high ✓), delete_task (medium ✗ should be high), delete_contact (high ✓), delete_opportunity (medium ✗ should be high). delete_task is medium but deletes a task from CRM — should be high. delete_opportunity is medium but irreversibly removes a deal — should be high. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/tasks.ts, opportunities.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] Bulk Operation Risk Tier Gaps** — bulk_pause_all (medium), bulk_resume_all (safe), bulk_reschedule_job (medium) are non-destructive but affect in-flight bulk message jobs. bulk_cancel_all (high) is correctly destructive. However, bulk_pause_all prevents 100k messages from sending — should this be high? Current classification is medium (requires med_and_high gate only). No strong issue but warrants review for consistency with bulk_cancel_all. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-management.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] No Tool Startup Validation or Dead Code Check** — TOOL_REGISTRY is built from ALL_ENTRIES (index.ts line 65-67) but no startup validation: no check that every tool has a unique name, valid handler, or that handlers reference actual GHL operations. If a tool is defined but never exported in a category array (CONTACTS_TOOLS, etc.), it silently doesn't get registered — no warning. Dead tools could accumulate. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:41-67)
- **[LOW] Confirmation Flag Not Stripped from Error Returns** — When executeTool() returns error (before handler), args.confirmed_by_rep is not stripped from the error context (args_preview in admin signals). If error is logged/signaled, it leaks that the tool required confirmation. Low risk (not user-facing) but inconsistent with line 233 stripping the flag. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:271-285 (admin signal recording))
- **[MEDIUM] Import Contact Tool (import_contacts_from_data) — High Risk but No Bulk Preview** — import_contacts_from_data is marked high risk (correct) but there is no preview tool like preview_bulk_message_v2 to show rep how many contacts will be imported and what data will be used. Rep confirms the tool call once, then potentially 1000 contacts are created. No 'confirm each batch' pattern. This is inconsistent with bulk_messages_v2 which requires preview + disclaimers. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/contacts.ts (import tool if exists, else bulk-messages-v2.ts pattern should apply))
- **[MEDIUM] Test Mode Gate Doesn't Mock Follow-up Operations** — Test mode (testSessionId check, line 197) mocks non-safe tools, returning {simulated:true}. However, if a tool creates a record (e.g., create_task) and returns ID in simulated mode, downstream tools might try to reference that fake ID (e.g., update_task with fake task_id). In test, subsequent updates would fail 'task not found' because the ID was never created. This is correct behavior (prevents unintended writes) but can make test flows confusing. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:197-209)

### Production blockers
- **[REFUTED/LOW] delete_appointment and delete_task Missing High Risk Classification** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: delete_appointment is safe but deletion of calendar slots is destructive (breaks customer communication). delete_task is medium but deletion is irreversible. Both should require confirmation gate. Current state: anyone can call these without 'Confirma?' verbal confirmation, risking accidental deletions.
  - Fix: Change delete_appointment risk from safe → high. Change delete_task risk from medium → high. Audit: search for all delete_* tools and verify they're high risk. Run test: confirm high-risk delete tools block without confirmed_by_rep flag.
  - Veredicto: 
src/lib/account-assistant/tools/calendar.ts:1425 — delete_appointment has risk: "high"
src/lib/account-assistant/tools/tasks.ts:216 — delete_task has risk: "high"
src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:211-229 — executeTool() enforces confirmation gate in CODE: "if (requiresConfirm && args.confirmed_by_rep !== true) return error"
src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:80-127 — withConfirmationParam() injects confirmed_by_rep as REQUIRED field in schema for risk="high" tools
src/lib/account-assistant/processor.ts — confirmationMode defaults to "high_only" (|| fallback on all callsites)
src/supabase/migrations/00069_confirmation_mode_default_high_only.sql — DB DEFAULT set to 'high_only'

Both tools are classified as risk="high" and are protected by a runtime enforcement gate (not just prompt instruction). When called without confirmed_by_rep=true, executeTool returns error status with message requiring re-call with flag=true.

- **[REFUTED/LOW] delete_opportunity Risk Level (medium → should be high)** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: Deleting an opportunity (deal) is irreversible and high-impact. Currently marked medium, so confirmation_mode='high_only' does NOT require confirmation. If rep or LLM calls this, opportunity is deleted without 'Confirma?' check.
  - Fix: Change delete_opportunity risk from medium → high. Test: rep in confirmation_mode='high_only' tries delete_opportunity → should block until confirmed.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/tools/opportunities.ts:401 — deleteOpportunity explicitly defined with risk: "high" (not medium). src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:213-216 — confirmation gate logic correctly evaluates: mode="high_only" AND risk="high" → requiresConfirm=true. Line 218-228 enforces gate: if requiresConfirm && args.confirmed_by_rep !== true, returns error blocking execution. Line 212 provides fallback: ctx.confirmationMode ?? "high_only" ensures even null/undefined confirmation_mode defaults to highest enforcement level.
- **[REFUTED/LOW] Confirmation Gate Not Enforced for Disabled Tools Edge Case** (conf: low)
  - Porquê: If admin disables a high-risk tool (e.g., send_message_to_contact) via agent_configs.disabled_tools, tool never reaches LLM. However, if tool is disabled VIA confirmation_mode override (not disabledNames), edge case could exist. Not a current blocker but risk vector if disabling logic changes.
  - Fix: Add test: admin disables send_message_to_contact → verify LLM never sees tool definition. Verify disabled tools don't appear in getAllToolDefinitions() output.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:139-163 — Both getAllToolDefinitions() and getToolDefinitions() filter disabled tools BEFORE applying confirmation_mode injection via withConfirmationParam(). Line 145: .filter((e) => !disabled.has(e.def.name)) happens before line 146: .map((e) => withConfirmationParam(...)). Same pattern in getToolDefinitions at lines 157-162. The confirmation_mode parameter only controls schema injection of the `confirmed_by_rep` field (line 103-127 in withConfirmationParam) — it does NOT re-add tools to the schema or bypass the disabled filter. There is no path where confirmation_mode can "disable via override" — confirmation_mode only controls GATE strictness (always/medium_and_high/high_only), not FILTER membership. Test coverage in scripts/test-tool-resolver.ts:43-50 explicitly validates "disabledTools tira tool liberada por módulo" — disabled tools are removed even when modules enable them. No cross-contamination between the two independent controls.
- **[PARTIAL/MEDIUM] Test Mode + Confirmation Gate Interaction Not Fully Tested** (conf: medium)
  - Porquê: Test mode gate (line 197) executes before confirmation gate (line 218). If testSessionId is set, high-risk tools return {simulated:true} without checking confirmed_by_rep. This is correct (test should not require real confirmation), but if test framework fails to set testSessionId, production gate applies. No integration test verifying both gates work together.
  - Fix: Add integration test: testSessionId=null, call high-risk tool without confirmed_by_rep → should block. Call WITH testSessionId → should mock. Verify both paths.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts:197 (test mode gate executes first with `if (ctx.testSessionId && ctx.testSessionId.length > 0 && risk !== "safe")` returning mock before line 218 confirmation gate check). This is CORRECT behavior — test mode intentionally bypasses confirmation. However: (1) No integration test exists covering test mode + confirmation gate interaction together. All scripts use testSessionId: null (smoke-test-h32.ts, e2e-pedro-test.ts, sanity-gustavo-tools.ts). (2) The test route (src/app/api/agents/account-assistant/test/route.ts:190) ALWAYS passes valid sessionId so "test framework fails to set" is imprecise — would only fail if route ITSELF broke. (3) Code is functionally safe: processor.ts:334 uses `||` and buildToolCtx uses `??`, both ensuring testSessionId is null if missing, not undefined.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] GHL ID Validation Regex May Accept Invalid IDs** (conf: low)
  - Porquê: validateGhlId() regex !/^[A-Za-z0-9]+$/ requires alphanumeric only, 18+ chars. This rejects legitimate GHL IDs with hyphens (though real GHL IDs are typically hex-looking), and might accept obviously fake patterns like '123456789012345678' (all digits, but length-only validation). LLM could pass a fake ID that passes validation but fails at GHL, wasting API call.
  - Fix: Review GHL API ID format spec. If GHL IDs are actually [A-Za-z0-9]+ fixed-length, add length bounds. Add test: pass fake IDs (e.g., 'aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa', '12345678901234567890') → confirm validation rejects or GHL API fails cleanly.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] No Startup Validation of Tool Registry Integrity** (conf: medium)
  - Porquê: TOOL_REGISTRY built at runtime from ALL_ENTRIES. No validation that: (1) all entries have unique names, (2) all have valid handlers, (3) no handlers are undefined, (4) risk field is one of [safe|medium|high]. If a tool is misconfigured, bug is silent until tool is called.
  - Fix: Add startup check in processor.ts or main app init: validate TOOL_REGISTRY via getTlRegistry(), assert all tools valid, log count. Example: `if (new Set(Object.keys(TOOL_REGISTRY)).size !== Object.keys(TOOL_REGISTRY).length) throw 'Duplicate tool names'`.


---

## Ferramentas — filter engine & bulk messages

Filter Engine is a universal DSL-based contact/opportunity query system (FEL — Filter Expression Language) with compiler, executor, and capability matrix. It handles AND/OR/NOT filters, alias resolution (stageName→stageId, custom field slugs), server-side/client-side op selection, pagination (5000 cap), and audit logging. Bulk Messages V2 uses it for multi-segment campaigns with tier-based disclaimers, rich interpolation ({first_name}, {tags[0]}, {custom.slug}), and delivery strategy computation. Infrastructure is production-ready but has edge case gaps and potential cross-location cache bleed under specific failure modes.

### Funcionalidades

**Filter Compiler (AND/OR/NOT AST) — 8/10**
- ✅ Recursive AST compilation with proper validation (depth cap 5, leaf cap 20). AND-of-leaves merge optimization (single GHL query vs N queries + intersection) prevents false negatives on limit-based intersects. Error handling with clear codes (INVALID_FEL, DEPTH_LIMIT, UNSUPPORTED_FIELD). Capability matrix decouples server vs client filtering strategy.
- ⚠️ NOT operator only works as inversion if leaf-level invertible (no complex NOT like NOT(field A OR field B)). Fallback to client-side pull-all is conservative but can truncate silently if cap hits before fetching full set.
- 🔧 Document NOT limitations in capability matrix and suggest LLM rewrites (e.g., NOT (A OR B) → NOT A AND NOT B). Emit warning in audit log when fallback-to-all triggers.

**Filter Executor & Paginación — 7/10**
- ✅ Proper pagination with cursor tracking (searchAfter for contacts V2, startAfterId for opps). Workspace isolation prevents set cross-contamination. Cap enforcement (5000 default, clamped 1-5000) with hit_safety_cap flag. Page size 100 is reasonable. Dedup in set operations (intersection/union) uses id-based Set for O(n) performance.
- ⚠️ Cap defensivo is per-execution, NOT per-request context (if caller calls filter 50 times in sequence, 50 × 5000 = 250k records possible). Pagination cursor anti-loop check (line 296) compares JSON.stringify(cursor) — could be fragile if cursor type changes. Client-side filter evaluation uses string toLowerCase() for comparison, but GHL field values might have encoding edge cases (accents, special chars).
- 🔧 Document cap behavior clearly (per-execution, not per-session). Use structured cursor comparison instead of JSON.stringify. Add validator for string comparisons in custom fields (Unicode normalization for Portuguese accents).

**Alias Resolution (stageName, customField, self) — 8/10**
- ✅ Rep-profile aliases expand textually before technical resolution (user says 'M2', bot has M2→'M2 dos 5 ao 20k', system resolves that to stageId). stageName resolver handles partial matches + exact matches with case-insensitive search. Custom field resolver checks fieldKey (slug), name, and ID (Pedro 2026-05-15). self/me/eu variants normalized. Stale-while-revalidate fallback if resolution fails.
- ⚠️ customField.slug → ID match has NO ambiguity detection (if 2 CFs have same slug, returns first match silently). stageName ambiguity raises error (good), but custom field doesn't — silent first-match can send to wrong field. looksLikeGhlUuid regex (/^[A-Za-z0-9]{18,}$/) is loose — GHL UUIDs are exactly 18-22 chars; could falsely match other strings.
- 🔧 Add ambiguity detection in customField resolver (error if 2+ CFs match slug). Tighten UUID regex to GHL spec. Cache warning in audit when ambiguous stageName detected.

**Cache (10min TTL, in-memory, per-location) — 6/10**
- ✅ Stale-while-revalidate gracefully serves old data if fetch fails (operational resilience). Separate cache entries per location (location_id:pipelines, location_id:customFields:contact, location_id:customFields:opportunity). invalidateLocation() and invalidateAll() provide manual control. Cache hits reduce GHL calls.
- ⚠️ **CRITICAL FOR MULTI-TENANT:** Single in-memory Map shared across ALL locations & all Node processes. If location A's pipelines fail to fetch, stale data from location A serves for 10min + all requests get same stale data (no isolation by tenant). No per-request context isolation — race between location A fetch + location B read could leak stage data. No cache size limit — pathological case (1000 locations × 50 CFs each = 50k entries) could cause memory bloat. TTL is fixed 10min regardless of staleness sensitivity (custom fields are mutable, pipelines static — should differ).
- 🔧 **URGENT:** Add tenant isolation (location_id as part of cache key — DONE — but validate no cross-location bleed in error paths). Add LRU eviction (50k entries max). Consider Redis for multi-process safety. Differentiate TTL by resource type (pipelines:30min, customFields:5min). Add cache hit/miss/stale metrics.

**Capability Matrix & Field Support — 7/10**
- ✅ Comprehensive documentation of server vs client ops per field (CONTACT_FIELDS, OPPORTUNITY_FIELDS both mapped). Empirical probe baseline (Gustavo 2026-05-14 + Pedro 2026-05-15 tests). Custom field fallback marked (server eq only, client-side other ops). Date field variance (dateAdded server gte/lte, dateOfBirth client-side only) explicitly noted. opportunity.monetaryValue marked as client-side after probe failure (was server param, now pulled via client filter).
- ⚠️ dateOfBirth has NO server-side support (probe 2026-05-14: 422 Invalid Operator) — but no audit alert when client-side fallback activates. monetaryValue server params deprecated (probe 2026-05-15) but comment says 'Confirmar periodicamente' — no automated probe re-run. opportunity.customField has NO GHL support but marked 'pull all + filter local' — can silently truncate 5000-cap if opp list > cap before filtering by CF.
- 🔧 Add warning flag in capability matrix for 'probe_needed_at' (dates when last confirmed). Implement scheduled probe job (weekly) to catch GHL API drift. Alert admin dashboard if monotonic counter of 'client_side_filter_applied' exceeds threshold (indicates capability drift).

**Disclaimers & Risk Tier — 8/10**
- ✅ Tier system (warm > 50, cold > 10) codified with clear thresholds. Four disclaimer types (lista_quente_required, risk_high_volume_warm, risk_any_volume_cold, first_bulk_ever) with required_flag enforcement. formatDisclaimersChecklist() consolidates 2+ disclaimers into single checklist (reduces turns — case Gustavo 2026-05-16 fix). Severity levels (info, warn, critical) guide display order.
- ⚠️ list_temperature detection is manual (bot asks 'warm/cold/unknown') — no heuristic from contact history (e.g., 'if lastActivity < 30d, assume warm'). first_bulk_ever detection ALWAYS shows (prior_bulks_count=0 hardcoded assumption) — no runtime detection if rep loaded from external system. Disclaimer ordering is defined but no visual priority in code (array order implicit).
- 🔧 Add heuristic inference of list_temperature from contact engagement (lastActivity, message_count in history). Wire prior_bulks_count detection from bulk_messages table. Make disclaimer severity sort explicit (critical first) in return data. Add A/B test flag for checklist vs separate formatting.

**Interpolation (Template Substitution) — 7/10**
- ✅ Rich placeholder support ({first_name}, {tags[0]}, {custom.slug}, {opportunity.stage_name}, {opportunity.customField.slug}). Three fallback modes (strict, empty, placeholder). parseTemplate() pre-validates placeholders (useful for preview). Custom field resolver with case-insensitive slug+name matching + self-reference. DATE custom fields convert timestamp ms → ISO → localize to pt-BR.
- ⚠️ Fallback='strict' leaves placeholder unreplaced + marks missing, but LLM still sends template to bulk dispatch (no pre-flight hard error, only warning). opportunity custom field resolver looks in active_opportunity.custom_fields ONLY — if contact has 0 open opps, all opp placeholders miss silently. PLACEHOLDER_REGEX is overly loose (allows any a-z_. — could match 'tags.foo' which doesn't exist). tags[N] out-of-bounds doesn't error, just returns undefined.
- 🔧 Add mode='fail_fast' that errors if any placeholder is missing (for strict bulk use cases). Infer opportunity from most-recent opp (open or won) if no active opp. Validate placeholder names against known schema (at parse time, not runtime). Document missing value behavior clearly in tool description.

**Bulk Messages V2 (Multi-Segment, Disclaimers, Delivery) — 7/10**
- ✅ Multi-segment dedup per contact_id across segments (default on). Delivery options pre-computed (auto/today/spread_days/custom_window) and presented as menu (reduces turns). F40 end_at clamped to 21:00 auto (no late-night spam risk). Active job coexistence detection + suggestion of start_after (estimated_completion_at). Cooldown warnings for contacts that already got bulk <24h (info-only, not blocking). Similar job detection (text similarity >0.7) to prevent duplication.
- ⚠️ Segments parameter allows max 10, but no warning if 10 segments have small overlaps — dedup math can be expensive (contact checked against ALL seen IDs per segment). resolution of segments calls executeContactsFilter with limit=5000 HARD (no override) — if user wants to bulk msg 20k contacts with custom cap, truncated silently. weekly_cap_warning is info-only but multi-segment job could exceed it if each segment passes daily but total > weekly — no validation in schedule, only preview warning.
- 🔧 Cap segment count at 5 (rare to need >5). Allow option.limit override in preview (document risk). Add hard validation in schedule (not just warning) if total_contacts + used_this_week > weekly_cap (option: confirm_exceed_weekly). Optimize dedup: use bloom filter or set-based intersect if segments > 3.

**Audit Log (filter_executions table) — 8/10**
- ✅ Fire-and-forget async insert (non-blocking). Comprehensive data: FEL input, plan_steps (each GHL call + params), applied_aliases, duration_ms, error_message, consumer_tool, ghl_calls_made. Indices on rep_id+created_at DESC, slow queries (>5s), consumer_tool. Cleanup job mentioned (30 day retention) — good for compliance.
- ⚠️ Audit insert catches errors and logs warning only (no retry). If Supabase is down, 0 audit trail for that execution (silent loss). Plan steps are JSON-serialized (no diffs stored) — can't detect if same FEL regressed in performance over time. No rate limit detection (if 1 rep fires 1k FEL queries in 1min, no alert).
- 🔧 Add retry logic (max 2 retries on transient error) for audit insert. Store previous plan_steps hash to detect perf regression. Add rate_limit_check (>100 FEL/min per rep = critical alert to admin). Archive to cold storage after 30 days (BigQuery or S3) for long-term audit.

**Error Handling & Retryability — 7/10**
- ✅ FilterEngineError with specific codes (INVALID_FEL, GHL_ERROR, ALIAS_NOT_FOUND, DEPTH_LIMIT, CAP_HIT). retryable flag in result (true for GHL_ERROR, false for validation). Compiler validates before execution (fails fast). Executor catches and wraps unexpected errors. Stale-while-revalidate fallback for cache misses.
- ⚠️ GHL_ERROR slices err.message to 200 chars (line 271) — might lose critical context. Custom field resolver has NO fallback if getCustomFields() fails with non-transient error (e.g., 404 if location has no CF endpoint) — just throws, request dies. Pagination loop exit condition uses JSON.stringify cursor comparison + undefined/null checks (lines 290-296) — if GHL returns cursor=0 (falsy but valid), could exit early.
- 🔧 Log full error to stdout before truncating for user message. Add cache fallback for customFields (e.g., empty map if fetch fails, sub-tool warns 'custom field filtering unavailable'). Use explicit cursor presence check (cursor !== undefined && cursor !== null) instead of truthiness.

### Structural issues
- **[HIGH] In-memory cache not multi-process safe** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts. Single global Map<> shared across all Node processes via require cache. In serverless (AWS Lambda) or load-balanced deployments, each container has separate cache — location A's 10min-old pipelines in Container 1 are not visible to Container 2. This causes intermittent 'field not found' errors when requests bounce between containers. Stale-while-revalidate masks the issue temporarily but doesn't solve it. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts (lines 26, 83, 183, 219-225))
- **[MEDIUM] Custom field resolution has no ambiguity handling or logging** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/resolvers.ts. resolveCustomFieldBySlug() (line 280) checks fieldKey + name + partial match but returns FIRST hit if multiple CFs match. No ambiguity error raised (unlike stageName resolver line 266-276). If admin creates 2 CFs with same slug, user intent is guessed silently. No audit entry of which CF ID was chosen. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/resolvers.ts (lines 280-313))
- **[MEDIUM] Bulk V2 segment resolution hardcodes limit=5000, not user-configurable** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts line 359. resolveSegments() calls executeContactsFilter() with hard limit: cap=5000. If user wants to bulk 50k contacts split into 5 segments (10k each), each segment truncates to 5000. No parameter to override cap for bulk use case (where user explicitly wants ALL contacts in list). Total contacts reported to user is wrong (shows 5k per segment, not 10k actual). (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts (line 359, resolveSegments parameter))
- **[MEDIUM] Weekly cap enforcement is info-only in schedule, no validation** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts. preview computes weekly_cap_warning (inforamtional), but schedule_bulk_message_v2 handler does not re-validate against weeklyCap. User can schedule 3 bulk jobs totaling > weekly_cap in same day; system accepts all 3 because daily cap is enforced per-job but weekly is not. (src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts (lines 452-458 preview, handler ~line 683 schedule — missing weeklyCap check))
- **[MEDIUM] Opportunity custom field filtering silently truncates results** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/capabilities.ts lines 231-243. opportunity.customField has no server-side support. Compiler generates client_side_filter on all opportunities (pulled via cap 5000). If location has 100k opps and filters by custom field, true result <1000 but returned truncated at 5000. complete flag set to false but user may miss 'why' (cap hit). No warning in tool description that opp custom field filtering is best-effort. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/capabilities.ts (lines 231-243), executor.ts (line 300 client_side_filter logic))
- **[MEDIUM] Filter execution audit insert is fire-and-forget, no retry** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/audit.ts line 25. Async insert in void IIFE with only console.warn on error. No retry logic, no alert to admin. If Supabase down, audit row is silently lost — compliance/troubleshooting gap. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/audit.ts (lines 25-61))
- **[LOW] dateOfBirth always triggers client-side fallback, not documented in tools** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/capabilities.ts line 127-133. dateOfBirth has no server-side support (GHL returns 422). Compiler generates pull-all + client-side filter (hits 5000 cap). Tool descriptions don't warn user about potential truncation. User unaware query filters AFTER cap applied. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/capabilities.ts (line 129), tool descriptions in bulk-messages-v2.ts (line 287))
- **[LOW] Pagination cursor comparison via JSON.stringify is fragile** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/executor.ts lines 296, 437. Pagination anti-loop uses JSON.stringify(cursor) === JSON.stringify(previous). If GHL returns cursor as [0] vs [0, ''] or different field order, stringify may differ even if logically same. Unlikely but edge case. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/executor.ts (lines 290-296, 435-438))
- **[LOW] UUID detection regex too loose, could match non-UUID strings** — File: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/resolvers.ts line 327. looksLikeGhlUuid(/^[A-Za-z0-9]{18,}$/) matches any 18+ alphanumeric string. GHL UUIDs are typically 18-22 chars. Could falsely match base-64 or other IDs. Low severity (rare collision) but should use GHL spec. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/resolvers.ts (line 327-329))
- **[LOW] No rate limiting on filter executions per rep/location** — Filter engine has no check for abuse (e.g., 1000 FEL queries in 1 minute = DDoS risk). Audit log captures it but no proactive throttle. Not critical for product but should have guardrails. (src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/executor.ts (no rate check))

### Production blockers
- **[REFUTED/LOW] Cache cross-location data bleed (multi-tenant isolation gap)** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: Single in-memory Map stores pipelines + customFields per location using location_id as part of the key (format: 'location_id:resource'). However, if location A's customFields fetch FAILS and returns stale data, the stale entry persists in the shared cache. A concurrent request for location B could theoretically access location A's stale custom fields if: (1) timing is tight, (2) location B shares no customFields, and (3) a fallback key lookup happens. While current code structure mitigates this via location_id:model keys, no test confirms isolation under error paths.
  - Fix: Add multi-tenant isolation test: (1) Mock cache as global, (2) Trigger CF fetch failure for location A, (3) Verify location B fetch doesn't return location A data. If bleed detected, add location_id validation in resolver before returning cached CF. Consider Redis instead of in-memory for multi-process safety.
  - Veredicto: 
src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts:28-29 — key() function uses location_id as MANDATORY part of cache key: `return '${location_id}:${resource}'`. Example: "ABC123:customFields:contact" vs "XYZ789:customFields:contact" — keys are completely different for different locations.

src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts:33-36 — getEntry() performs EXACT Map.get() lookup: `const entry = cache.get(k)`. No fallback, no wildcard, no prefix matching. Different location IDs produce different keys, lookup always retrieves data for the correct location or returns null.

src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts:152,154,186 — fetchCustomFieldsByModel() uses SAME key 'k' for both fresh check (line 154) and stale-while-revalidate fallback (line 186). When fetch fails, `cache.get(k)` on line 186 retrieves stale data using IDENTICAL location_id:resource key. No cross-location lookup exists.

src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts:219-220 — invalidateLocation() iterates `cache.keys()` with prefix matching (`k.startsWith()`) but is only called during cache invalidation (explicit admin action), never during normal data retrieval path.

Claim allegation of "fallback key lookup" has NO CODE EVIDENCE. All cache operations use exact matching via Map.get(k) where k includes location_id. Code inspection finds ZERO instances of wildcard lookup, secondary fallback, or cross-tenant key resolution in the cache retrieval path.

Concurrent request isolation verified: Thread 1 for location A accesses "LOC_A:customFields:contact", Thread 2 for location B accesses "LOC_B:customFields:contact". Different keys, separate cache entries, no cross-contamination possible.

Decision code H27 (2026-05-15) in docs/DECISIONS.md documents cache design with 10min TTL for pipelines + customFields per location. No known multi-tenant isolation gap is recorded.

- **[REFUTED/LOW] Unvalidated custom field resolver ambiguity in bulk messages** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: customField slug resolver (resolveCustomFieldBySlug in resolvers.ts, line 280) returns FIRST match if multiple CFs have same slug — no ambiguity detection unlike stageName. If admin somehow creates two custom fields with identical slugs (name + fieldKey), bulk message interpolation silently picks the first, sending {custom.ambiguous_field} to wrong field. No audit trail of which CF ID was chosen.
  - Fix: In resolveCustomFieldBySlug, collect ALL matches (not just first). If matches.length > 1, throw FilterEngineError with 'ALIAS_AMBIGUOUS'. Or, log ambiguity event in audit table with both CF IDs + notify admin dashboard. Test with schema that has duplicate slug.
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/resolvers.ts:280-313 — resolveCustomFieldBySlug searches in sequential passes (exact fieldKey, exact name, partial name), each returning on first match of that pass. However, GHL API guarantees uniqueness of fieldKey per location/model (per _planning/ghl-api-reference.md: "Field key... uniquely identifies"). The stageName ambiguity detection (lines 266-276) is architecturally correct because stages genuinely can be ambiguous across pipelines; custom fields cannot be. buildCustomFieldResolver (interpolator.ts:202-224) builds Map<string,string> (slug→id), but Map.set on duplicate key is safe-by-design because duplicates cannot occur from GHL API. No production blocker—code correctly relies on GHL API constraint rather than defending against impossible scenario.
- **[CONFIRMED/HIGH] Weekly cap only warning in bulk preview, no hard validation in schedule** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: preview_bulk_message_v2 computes weekly_cap_warning (inform-only) but schedule_bulk_message_v2 does not validate against weeklyCap before inserting recipients. If rep has 1000-per-week cap and sends 3 daily jobs (500 each) on same day, the third job inserts successfully even though total > 1000/week. Weekly usage counter only checked during preview, not at job creation time.
  - Fix: In schedule_bulk_message_v2 handler, after resolving segments, call getWeeklyCap() + countRecipientsLast7Days(). If total_contacts + used_last_7d > weeklyCap, either: (a) error with option to confirm_exceed_weekly flag, or (b) trim recipients to fit cap (with audit note). Match behavior of daily cap enforcement (which IS hard in schedule via getDailyCap).
  - Veredicto: /Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts:445-458 (preview warning is "heads-up", schedule is "source of truth" — false); line 806-820 (weekly cap check without transaction/lock); line 1024-1135 (insert happens after check, race window); /Users/pedropoleza/SPARK APPS/AI platform/supabase/migrations/00066_bulk_smart_cap_and_priority.sql:58-66 (weekly_bulk_message_cap added to DB schema but NO constraint/trigger to enforce)
- **[PARTIAL/MEDIUM] opportunity.customField server-side unsupported, client-side pullall can exceed cap** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: Capability matrix notes opportunity.customField as 'server-side endpoint = none' — GHL /opportunities/search doesn't accept custom field filters. Engine pulls ALL opportunities (with cap 5000) then client-side filters by CF. If location has 100k opps and user filters by opp.customField = 'high_priority', result set is truncated to 5000 opps BEFORE the custom field filter applies. Real result might be 20 opps but system returns 'complete=false', misleading the user.
  - Fix: Add audit log warning when opportunity.customField filter is applied (action='client_side_filter' + field starts with 'opportunity.customField'). In executor, adjust complete flag: if client-side filter was applied to opps, return complete=false + hit_safety_cap=true always. Document in tool description that opp custom field filtering is advisory (may truncate unexpectedly).
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/capabilities.ts:232-243 marks opportunity.customField with server_side_endpoint="none" and empty server_side_ops array. src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/compiler.ts:254-277 checks (isOppField && supportsServer); when supportsServer=false for opp.customField, falls through to Case 3 (line 279-309) which generates opportunities_search (no CF filter) + client_side_filter. src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/executor.ts:355-445 (paginateOpportunitiesSearch) pulls opportunities up to cap=5000 (line 440-443), sets workspace.any_truncated=true (line 441), and records totalReported from first page meta.total (line 409-411) BEFORE cap is applied. Line 118 computes complete = !workspace.any_truncated && trimmed.length === finalSet.length, so complete will be false when cap is hit. The return result (line 124-129) includes both total_reported_by_ghl (ground truth ~100k) and complete=false, which correctly signals truncation but the data was filtered AFTER truncation, not before.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Audit insert fire-and-forget, no retry or loss alert** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: auditFilterExecution (audit.ts line 25) spawns async insert via createAdminClient() in a void IIFE — no error handling beyond console.warn. If Supabase is temporarily down, audit row silently drops. No metrics track audit loss. In production, this creates compliance gap (compliance team cannot audit bulk message activity if inserts fail).
  - Fix: Implement 2-retry logic with exponential backoff (initial 1s, then 3s). If all retries fail, emit critical log + PushNotification to admin. Or queue audit in local SQLite if Supabase unavailable (sync on recovery). Track audit_insert_failures counter.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] dateOfBirth operator fallback not clearly marked in tool descriptions** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: getFieldCapability() returns dateOfBirth with server_side_ops=[] and client_side_ops=['eq', 'neq', 'before', 'after', ...], but tool descriptions (get_contacts_filtered, describe_filter_capabilities) do not call out that dateOfBirth ALWAYS triggers pull-all + client-side filter, potentially truncating silently. User unaware query on 20k-contact location filters after 5000-item cap.
  - Fix: In tool description for get_contacts_filtered / describe_filter_capabilities, add explicit warning: 'dateOfBirth filtering pulls all contacts (may hit 5000 safety cap). For better performance, use dateAdded or lastActivity if possible.' Include similar warning in plan step output (audit log when client_side_filter action on dateOfBirth).
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Pagination cursor anti-loop check uses JSON.stringify (fragile)** (conf: ?)
  - Porquê: Executor lines 296 & 437: if (JSON.stringify(next) === JSON.stringify(cursor)) break; — if GHL returns cursor as [0, 'id'] sometimes and [0] other times (array length varies), stringify comparison could incorrectly think they're different when logically identical. Or if GHL returns cursor with fields in different order, stringify differs but value is same.
  - Fix: Replace JSON.stringify comparison with structural equality function (e.g., deepEqual). Or use GHL's cursor type directly (likely string startAfterId) and compare primitives. Test with locations that have cursor of different shapes.


---

## Planejamento — planos vs implementado

The Spark AI Hub codebase has extensive planning documentation (DECISIONS.md with 35+ decision codes H/C/P/NB, plus 8 major feature plans from 2026-05-15 onwards). Core SparkBot functionality (rep-facing) is largely implemented with robust error handling and multi-layer idempotency. However, the lead-facing platform (sales/recruitment/custom agents) exists in multiple development states: the modular platform (H35) is in Phases 0-1 (foundational/rep-facing), while Etapa 4 (Prospecção/prospecting 2.0) has 8 major UI+runner features split across flag-gated runners. Critical gaps exist in UI completeness, feature flag defaults being OFF in production, and missing smoke validation before production release.

### Funcionalidades

**SparkBot (Account Assistant) — Rep-Facing Core — 8/10**
- ✅ 88 tools fully implemented with confirmation gates (H8). Multi-layer idempotency (7 layers in CLAUDE.md). Robust error handling: C14-C23 calendar bugs fixed. Timezone-aware scheduling (C14b). Proactive rules partially implemented (daily briefing working, others scaffolded). WhatsApp delivery via Stevo + GHL fallback (C1 fixed). Billing with hard cap enforcement (H18, C13 schema fixed).
