### Structural issues
- **[LOW] Dead Code + Deprecated Tools in Schema — Technical Debt** — Bulk V1 tools (schedule_bulk_message, preview_bulk_message) marked deprecated in descriptions (⚠️ DEPRECATED in prompt-builder.ts tool descriptions) but NOT removed from schema. Tools still callable by LLM. V1 helpers preserved (countRecipientsLast24h, etc.) but code has duplication vs V2. Recommendation: either (a) remove V1 tools entirely + migrate any remaining V1 usages to V2, or (b) keep as compat layer but document clearly. Currently limbo state creates confusion (LLM may pick wrong tool). Files: account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages.ts (V1) vs bulk-messages-v2.ts (V2). (/src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages.ts, /src/lib/account-assistant/tools/bulk-messages-v2.ts, /src/lib/account-assistant/prompt-builder.ts)
- **[MEDIUM] Timezone Logic Scattered + Risk of Regression — C14-C23 Fixes** — Calendar tools (list_my_free_slots, block_calendar_slot, createAppointment, updateAppointment) have complex timezone handling. Multiple fixes applied (C14-C23: calendarHasOpenHoursAt UTC→local, listMyFreeSlots event handling, startOfDayInTz offset calc, INTERSECT-conservador heuristic, overnight calendars, hardened parsing). Despite fixes, each function has its own tz logic. Intl.DateTimeFormat used inconsistently (sometimes with timeZone param, sometimes not). Risk: future GHL calendar changes or edge cases (DST transitions, calendar deletion race) could re-introduce bugs. Tests exist (C14: 8 unit tests pass) but coverage may not be exhaustive. (/src/lib/account-assistant/tools/calendar.ts (lines ~700-1000), /src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/reminder-runner.ts (computeNextRun timezone logic))
- **[MEDIUM] Modular Platform Phases 1-2 Code Paths Experimental — Rollback Risk** — AGENT_MOTOR_UNIFIED flag toggles between old OpenAI path (queue-processor legacy) and new motor (assembler.ts). Both paths co-exist in codebase. Parity tests (test-motor-parity.ts, test-sales-parity.ts) pass but flags default OFF. If flag flipped to ON without staged rollout, risk of: (1) undiscovered incompatibilities in assembler delegation, (2) tool resolver not filtering correctly per audience, (3) lead-facing module composition (test-lead-compose.ts) untested E2E. Rollback would require flipping flag back + potential data corruption if entitlements or prompt overrides written during ON state. (/src/lib/agent-platform/assembler.ts, /src/lib/queue/queue-processor.ts:~80-140, /scripts/test-motor-parity.ts, /scripts/test-sales-parity.ts)
- **[HIGH] Feature Flags All OFF by Default — Runners Dormant** — Three major prospecting features (outreach, sequences, recurring) have runners implemented but entry points check env flags: OUTREACH_RUNNER_ENABLED, BULK_SEQUENCES_ENABLED, RECURRING_CAMPAIGNS_ENABLED. All default to empty string (false). Cron /api/cron/sparkbot-proactive wires calls to these runners (lines 223-292) but with flags OFF, early returns happen. Without flags set, no campaigns dispatchable. .env.example documents flags but doesn't enable them. Risk: admin forgets to set flags, campaigns sit pending indefinitely, rep confusion ('where's my campaign?'). Mitigation: either (a) enable flags by default + gate behind UI toggle per agente, or (b) document flag requirement + add warning to admin dashboard when flags OFF. (/src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/outreach-runner.ts:~20-30, /src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/sequence-runner.ts:~20-30, /src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/recurring-runner.ts:~20-30, /src/app/api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:~272-292)
- **[HIGH] Reactive Polling Rules Incomplete — Opportunity.Stale et al. Stubbed** — Planning defines 10 reactive polling rule types. Implementation: only 'daily briefing' fully coded. Reactive polling function (processReactivePolling, route.ts:203) returns stub `{fired:0, skipped:0}`. Rules like 'opportunity_stale', 'task_due_soon', 'contact_inactive', 'inbound_unanswered' are defined in schema (assistant_proactive_rules with rule_type='reactive') but handlers not implemented. When cron tries to fire them, function returns empty result. Risk: V3 promise of 'system-initiated proactive messages' unfulfilled; reps won't get appointment reminders, opportunity decay alerts, etc. (/src/app/api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:~203-207 (stub), /src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/daily-briefing.ts (example implementation to port))
- **[MEDIUM] Prospecting UI Wizard Steps Incomplete — Etapa 4.1 Unfinished** — Campaign creation wizard (planned Etapa 4.1, steps 1-6) is scaffolded but missing key steps: step 2 (filter selection via FEL), step 4 (delivery strategy picker), step 5 (disclaimers review), step 6 (final review + schedule). Detail view has TODO comment for 'recipients table com pagina'. A/B variant stats not rendered. Recurring campaign UI missing cron picker (just accepts free-form string). These gaps mean campaigns can be created but user experience is minimal/broken. Admin will create campaigns but stats/management incomplete. (/src/app/hub/campaigns/new/page.tsx (scaffold), /src/app/hub/campaigns/[id]/detail-view.tsx (TODOs), /src/lib/hub/campaigns.ts (preview/schedule endpoints))
- **[MEDIUM] Entitlement Gate Incomplete — Tool Filtering by Audience Not Wired** — Agent entitlement (H35, agent-platform/entitlements.ts) checks if location+capability granted (default OFF log-first). Tool resolver (tool-resolver.ts) exists but tool filtering per audience (rep-facing vs lead-facing) + entitlement not fully integrated into dispatcher or queue-processor. Tools are registered globally; no enforcement of 'this tool only available to lead_facing agentes' at runtime. Risk: admin creates lead-facing agente without entitlement, grants entitlement later, tools not available until app restart. Or rep-facing agente somehow calls lead-facing tool (RBAC bypass). (/src/lib/agent-platform/entitlements.ts, /src/lib/agent-platform/tool-resolver.ts, /src/lib/account-assistant/tools/index.ts (registry), /src/lib/agent-platform/assembler.ts (resolver integration gap))
- **[LOW] Lead History Cache 5min May Stale — No Refresh Mechanism** — F37 lead-history loader caches contact history + opp data for 5min (cache.ts). If contact replies or opp moves stage within 5min, agent doesn't see update until cache expires. No manual refresh endpoint for rep (e.g., 'refresh lead data' command). Risk: agent makes decision based on stale data (e.g., opp thought to be in 'pitch' but moved to 'won' 2 min ago). Mitigation: document cache TTL in prompt, add optional '/refresh' command handler. (/src/lib/queue/lead-history.ts:~60-80, /src/lib/account-assistant/filter-engine/cache.ts (similar pattern))
- **[LOW] Custom Keywords for Handoff Not Admin-Configurable — Hardcoded Keywords** — F37 should-respond.ts checks hardcoded keywords ('can you get me a human', 'falar com um agente', etc.) + generic heuristics (last inbound age, opp status). Admin cannot customize keywords per location/language. Risk: international deployments (Spanish 'atendente', Portuguese variations) may miss handoff trigger. Mitigation: move keywords to agent_configs.handoff_policy.custom_keywords_handoff (array, D3 pending decision), add UI in settings. (/src/lib/queue/should-respond.ts:~30-60, /src/types/agent.ts (handoff_policy type))
- **[LOW] Bulk Runner Health Monitoring Only Signal-Based — No UI** — H32.5 bulk-runner-health-check.ts monitors for stale bulk jobs (no progress >5min) and signals admin. But there's no UI in /hub to view runner health status or manually trigger 'run now'. Admin only sees signals if error occurs. Rep has no visibility. Mitigation: add /hub/campaigns section for 'runner health' (last_tick_at, last_error, consecutive_errors, is_stale), expose via GET /api/hub/bulk-runner/health. (/src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/bulk-runner-health-check.ts, /src/app/api/admin/cron-health/route.ts (exposes via admin API), missing: /src/app/api/hub/bulk-runner/health/route.ts)

### Production blockers
- **[CONFIRMED/HIGH] Core Proactive Rules Incomplete — Reactive Polling Stubbed** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: Planning doc (ultra-review-findings.md, §6 + DECISIONS.md) defines 10 reactive polling types (appointment_upcoming, post_meeting, task_due_soon, task_overdue, inbound_unanswered, contact_inactive, opportunity_stale, deal_won, etc.) needed for V3 launch. Codebase has scaffolding in /api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:203-207 (`processReactivePolling` returns empty stub) and only 'daily briefing' fully implemented. Without reactive rules, V3 (real WhatsApp dispatch) has only reminder-scheduler (rep-initiated) working; system-initiated proactivity is absent.
  - Fix: Implement each reactive rule type in a dedicated handler function (appointment_upcoming: query calendar events in future window, generate context, dispatch. Etc.) Port the pattern from daily-briefing.ts (loadDailyContext + buildPrompt + dispatchRule). Wrap each in try-catch + signal admin on failure. Wire in processReactivePolling loop. Add feature flag per rule type for staged rollout. Test against real GHL data.
  - Veredicto: src/app/api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:422-431 — processReactivePolling function only implements post_meeting event; all others return {fired:0, skipped:0} on line 431. Code comment lines 418-420 states remaining events "ainda são stub". src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/system-rules.ts:22-244 shows all 10 rules seeded with full prompt templates but 9 are non-functional at runtime. _planning/ultra-review-findings.md:277 in Gap Analysis section §6 lists these 10 events as "🔴 CRÍTICO" item #1 required for V3 launch with 6-8h effort estimate.
- **[PARTIAL/MEDIUM] Prospecting 2.0 Feature Flags All OFF — Runners Dormant in Production** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: Etapa 4 (Prospecting 2.0) promises outreach, bulk sequences, recurring campaigns, A/B, opt-outs. All 3 runner functions (outreach-runner, sequence-runner, recurring-runner) check `process.env.OUTREACH_RUNNER_ENABLED !== '1'` (and variants) at entry, returning early if false. Flags default to empty string (OFF) in .env.example. Without setting flags, no campaigns fire. Etapa 4 estimated 8-10 sessions; UI only ~30% done. Cron wire-up exists (lines 272-292 in sparkbot-proactive route) but is no-op with flags OFF.
  - Fix: After completing Etapa 4.1-2 UI (campaigns list, new wizard, outreach config in agent detail) and smoke validation (create campaign → verify dispatch → check progress), set flags: export OUTREACH_RUNNER_ENABLED=1, BULK_SEQUENCES_ENABLED=1, RECURRING_CAMPAIGNS_ENABLED=1 in deployment. Document flag flip in release notes + add monitoring alert for runner errors. Provide admin dashboard to view runner health (missing: no UI yet for runner health, only signal on stale).
  - Veredicto: outreach-runner.ts:177, sequence-runner.ts:66, recurring-runner.ts:60 — all three runners check env flags and return early (no-op) if unset. .env.example:73-75 shows flags undefined (default OFF). .env.local (lines 1-38) does NOT contain any of the three flags, confirming OFF in current deployment. route.ts:272-292 wires all three into cron correctly; they execute but return zeros when flags are OFF. CatOutreach (agent-detail-view.tsx:1405-1468) is fully implemented, /hub/campaigns page exists (campaigns/page.tsx), contradicting "UI only ~30% done" — UI is 80%+ complete. Runners are fully implemented (not stubs); they're disabled-by-default for safety, not "dormant" or incomplete.
- **[REFUTED/LOW] Agent Modular Platform Motor OFF — Lead-Facing Uses Old Pipeline** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: H35 Plataforma Modular split into Phases. Phase 1 (motor unificado, 4 modules decomposed, parity tests) is done + gated behind AGENT_MOTOR_UNIFIED flag (default OFF). Queue-processor.ts line 137 checks the flag; if OFF, uses old LLM path (openai-client). F37 (Lead Awareness) depends on motor being ON (uses lead-history.ts + should-respond.ts in queue-processor). Riscos residuais in V2 report (#1): 'Re-run do coherence gate nunca rodou E2E com LLM+tools reais' — parity tests pass but real E2E not validated. Flipping to ON risks breaking lead-facing with no rollback plan.
  - Fix: Before flipping AGENT_MOTOR_UNIFIED=1 in prod: (1) Run E2E conversation test with motor ON (both Claude path + tool calling) vs OFF (old OpenAI path) side-by-side. (2) Check coherence gate re-run path (dispatcher.ts calls executeActions which calls executeTool → if tool fails, re-run gate triggers; validate this flow with mock failure). (3) Staged rollout: set flag to '0.01' (1%) in production, monitor execution_log for errors 24h before bumping to 100%. (4) Have rollback plan (disable flag immediately if coherence_gate_error or sales_turn_failure spike). Communicate change in release notes.
  - Veredicto: Queue-processor.ts:776-839 loads F37 (lead_history + should_respond) WITHOUT checking AGENT_MOTOR_UNIFIED flag. F37 is gated only by config.lead_history_config.enabled and config.handoff_policy.enabled, not by motor flag. Both code paths (motor ON/OFF) at lines 870-876 pass same promptCtx with leadHistory to either assembleSystemPrompt or buildSystemPrompt. Both functions include buildLeadHistorySection at sales-prompt-builder.ts:123. Test-sales-parity.ts confirms motor ON produces byte-identical output to legacy for lead-facing (5/5 passing). The referenced "E2E never ran" risk in _planning/_review-2026-05-19/RELATORIO-FINAL-V2.md refers to SparkBot coherence gate (account-assistant), not lead-facing. Motor is flag-gated with default OFF, rollback trivial. No technical dependency prevents activating motor for lead-facing.
- **[REFUTED/LOW] WhatsApp V3 Real Mode Not Implemented — V2 is Simulated-Only** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: CLAUDE.md and ultra-review (§6 'Gap Analysis V2 → V3') document V3 WhatsApp real mode as prerequisite. Dispatcher.ts:267-272 defines mode parameter ('simulated' vs 'real') but 'real' path just logs warning (stub). Cron route.ts:38 comment says 'Em V3+ WhatsApp envia direto. Em V2 é simulated'. Reminder-runner checks `if (!session_id && mode_real) {...}` but mode_real is hardcoded false for V2. Lead-facing (Etapa 6.1, §6 gap) depends on WhatsApp real delivery to actually contact leads.
  - Fix: Implement real WhatsApp send in dispatcher.ts by extending GHLClient.sendConversationMessage or equivalent for Hub location + contact → WhatsApp (or fallback SMS per outbound-channel routing). Test with evolution/Stevo integration (already handling inbound). Wire mode='real' in proactive rule dispatch + cron. Leave as V3 TODO but document clearly in release notes + code comment that WhatsApp real is future (Fase 2/3).
  - Veredicto: src/lib/account-assistant/proactive/dispatcher.ts:530-565 — mode='real' is FULLY IMPLEMENTED and actively dispatches via deliverProactiveMessage (imported from whatsapp-delivery.ts). The implementation sends messages via Stevo (primary) with GHL fallback, persists in sparkbot_messages, tracks delivery status, handles silence gates, and records billing. Commits show this was implemented 2026-05-04 (7d8349a) and is deployed on main branch. src/app/api/cron/sparkbot-proactive/route.ts:171-176 and 540-556 show BOTH scheduled rules ('Resumo matinal') and reactive rules ('post_meeting') actively call dispatchRule with mode='real'. whatsapp-delivery.ts:105-464 shows complete implementation with opt-in checks, Stevo integration, fallback to GHL API, hub resolution (multi-tenant aware), and metadata tracking. The claim incorrectly references the OLD cron comment (line 36-38) that says 'Em V3 é simulated em V2' but that is OUTDATED documentation — the actual code path runs real delivery. Reminder-runner.ts does NOT hardcode mode_real false; it uses deliverProactiveMessage (the shared helper) and respects silence gates appropriately per task_type. The comment at line 5-7 about 'WhatsApp (V3)' is context documentation, not indicative of stub code.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Etapa 1 Gaps Not Closed — Footgun UX Issues Remain** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: Etapa 1 (§3 in _gaps-prospeccao-2026-05-28/PLANO.md) has 10 ALTA gaps: 4 wizard fields missing (conversation_examples, greeting_style, persona_description, composer override), 4 detail-view dead fields (ai_model not editable, fallback_model no UI, disabled_tools no UI, system_prompt_override no UI), 2 footguns (0 channels no warning, timezone no validation). Etapa 2 has 8 MÉDIA gaps (KB wizard, outreach params, footgun outreach config, etc.). These are marked 'bloqueiam cutover' per Etapa 1 summary. Without them, admin creates broken agents (0 channels = silent failure) or loses settings (wizard → detail-view parity gaps).
  - Fix: Prioritize Etapa 1 footgun fixes before release: (1) Add red card warning if agent has 0 channels in CatChannel. (2) Add timezone <select> with IANA list validation in settings form. (3) Wire conversation_examples + greeting_style + persona_description in wizard (skippable nodes). (4) Make ai_model, fallback_model, disabled_tools editable in detail-view CatLimits. (5) Smoke: create agent via wizard → edit in detail-view → verify all fields persist. (6) Cover gaps 1.4.1-1.4.4 (truncations) by adding 'Ver tudo' links + pagination.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Lead Awareness (F37) Blocked by Motor Flag — Handoff UI Incomplete** (conf: med)
  - Porquê: F37 (Lead Awareness + Handoff, DECISIONS.md entry + F37 full doc) implements lead history loading (lead-history.ts), should-respond decision (should-respond.ts), handoff notification (handoff-notify.ts). Pipeline integrates in queue-processor.ts but is gated behind line 213: `if (AGENT_MOTOR_UNIFIED)` check (not explicit in code but depends on assembler which uses motor). Without motor ON, lead-facing agents don't load lead history → should-respond skipped → handoff never triggers. F37 UI (lead history config toggle, custom keywords, handoff notification settings) NOT built in /hub agent detail-view (no 'Memória do lead' Cat).
  - Fix: F37 is 'nice-to-have' for Fase 1 (sales with history improves but not critical). Gate behind feature flag `LEAD_AWARENESS_ENABLED` (default OFF) independently of motor. Wire UI toggle in detail-view (if lead_facing agente + lead_awareness_enabled). Test with 1 location + Alves Cury pilot. Document limitation: 'Lead history available for sales/recruitment; requires GHL read access on conversations endpoint'.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] Prospecting UI ~30% Complete — Etapa 4 Scope Unfeasible for Go-Live** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: Etapa 4 (Prospecting 2.0) planned as 8 sub-features (4.1 'Campanhas UI', 4.2 'Outreach config UI', 4.3 'Outreach runner', 4.4 'Sequência multi-toque', 4.5 'Recorrência', 4.6 'Segmentos dinâmicos', 4.7 'A/B', 4.8 'Whitelist'). Runners 3-8 exist (code present, flag-gated OFF). UI for 4.1-2 minimally sketched—campaign list page exists, detail page has TODO for recipients table, new campaign wizard missing steps 2-6 (filter selection, template, delivery, disclaimers, review). A/B stats not built. Recurring cron picker not implemented. Estimated 8-10 sessions remaining; scope too large for current timeline.
  - Fix: DO NOT attempt full Etapa 4 before go-live. Instead: (1) Keep runners flag-gated OFF in production. (2) Complete only Etapa 4.1 (Campanhas list + basic detail view) as UI skeleton. (3) Document 'Campaigns coming Q3' in release notes. (4) Plan Etapa 4.2-8 for post-launch (1-2 months). Alternatively, focus on Etapa 4.3 (outreach runner only, no UI) + smoke test, leave UI for Phase 2. This splits work manageable chunks.
- **[NÃO-VERIFICADO] V2 Smoke Test Risks #1, #3 Not Fully Mitigated — Coherence + Dupla-Resposta** (conf: high)
  - Porquê: V2 report (RELATORIO-FINAL-V2.md, §'Riscos residuais') identifies 4 risks. Risk #1: 'Re-run do coherence gate nunca rodou E2E com LLM+tools reais'. Coherence gate (dispatcher.ts, rerun path) catches hallucinations (bot says 'done' without running tool) but path only tested in unit tests (golden 49/49) not with real Claude API + tools + real GHL. Risk #3: 'Dupla-resposta conversacional' mitigated only while Stevo-only (WhatsApp API off). Dedup-guard by content (webhook-handler.ts, layer 8) implemented (atômico lock, re-check age) but never tested under concurrent webhook fire (e.g., 2 Stevo + 1 GHL same msg simultaneously).
  - Fix: Smoke plan (V2 report §'Plano de deploy'): Before prod deploy, test (1) coherence gate re-run with intentional tool failure (mock 403 from GHL contact endpoint) → verify bot re-tries AND doesn't say 'done' without actual write. (2) Dupla-resposta: send same message from 2 webhook sources simultaneously (simulate Stevo + GHL race) → verify only 1 processed, other locked out. (3) Sentinel monitoring: set up alert for 'coherence_gate_rerun' + 'webhook_dedup_lock' in admin_signals, monitor 1 hour post-deploy. If alert fires >N times, rollback.
